  830 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     73 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/6418               | * We use a traditional Bresenham run-length approach.
  831 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     74 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/6418               | * Run-slicing is possible, but the code is larger
  832 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     75 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/6418               | * and the increased cost means it's only valuable
  833 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     76 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/6418               | * for longer lines.  An optimal solution would switch
  834 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     77 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/6418               | * approaches based on line length.
  835 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     78 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/6418               | *
  836 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     79 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/6418               | * Start by identifying where x0 or x1 is on the
  837 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     80 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/6418               | * left.  To make life simpler we always work from
  838 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     81 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/6418               | * left to right, flipping the coordinates if
  839 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     82 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/6418               | * needed.
  840 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     83 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/6418               | *
  841 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     84 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/6418               | * We also need to figure out if the line is more
  842 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     85 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/6418               | * than 255 pixels long -- which, because of
  843 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     86 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/6418               | * inclusive coordinates, means abs(x0-x1) > 254.

 1391 |  3 FDRAW.CIRCLE.s     55 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/66BE               | * can extend off the edge.
 1392 |  3 FDRAW.CIRCLE.s     56 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/66BE               | *
 1393 |  3 FDRAW.CIRCLE.s     57 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/66BE               | * The computed values are stored in the rasterization
 1394 |  3 FDRAW.CIRCLE.s     58 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/66BE               | * tables.  For an outline circle, we also plot the
 1395 |  3 FDRAW.CIRCLE.s     59 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/66BE               | * points immediately.
